<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者心中這樣作意：為了尊敬的師長，應該將對方殺掉。或者認為：天都是世間的主人，世間是由他們所生的，如果有毀謗欲天、梵天等，應該將對方殺掉；或者是罵婆羅門，毀謗婆羅門種性的人，殺害毀謗者是合道理的，這是種族歧視的情況。這些為了尊長、或錯誤信仰、或種族歧視等動機而殺生，是與愚癡煩惱相應而引起殺生的第二種情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、由勸行殺2　午一、舉成殺業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種由勸行殺，由於他人的勸告而殺生，分二科；第一科舉成殺業，說明成就殺業的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或計殺生作及增長無異熟果，為他開演勸行殺業，彼由勸故，遂行殺事。時彼勸者所得殺罪，從癡所生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是指鼓勵他人殺生也是有罪的。或者愚癡執著殺生，做了殺生業，內心又不斷尋思殺生使殺業繼續增長，認為殺生不會招感異熟果，不會墮到地獄去，就告訴他人：殺生沒罪，教導他人去殺生，例如教人開海鮮店等，認為有錢賺就好，不會到地獄、沒那麼嚴重，佛教的法師亂說，不要相信，世間人錢比較重要。世間人有時候會這樣想。對方被他說動了，就很安心的去做殺生的事。這種勸告他人殺生所得殺罪，是由愚癡引發殺生的第三種情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例餘業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘業道，其餘不與取等業道也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此後所說從癡所生殺業道理，諸餘業道乃至邪見，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此後所說從癡所生殺生業的道理，其他不與取業道乃至邪見，道理也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、妄計方便</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科妄計方便，虛妄的執著方便而殺生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有妄計以其父母親愛眷屬擲置火中、斷食、投巖、棄於曠野，是真正法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有的人虛妄的執著將自己的父母，及親愛的眷屬等，放到火裡面燒掉，或令他們斷食而死，或將他們推下山谷，或丟棄到曠野，認為這是如法的事。這是由愚癡產生殺生的第四種情況。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》說：印度有一個國家，共同制訂一種法，如果父母眷屬老年將死的時候，就將他們放到火坑裡，或拋棄到曠野中讓他們自然死亡。以前看到讀者文摘報導愛斯基摩人的情況，人老的時候知道自己要快死時，就走到外面土坑裡，躺在那裡等死。這種情況從古代到現在都還有，老了就沒有用，要死了，乾脆將他放在將死的地方，這種事也是殺生。正確的態度是要照顧到最後一刻，親人的壽命沒有結束以前，不可以將他丟棄。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是一切，名癡所生殺生業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說為由祠祀福、為尊長等、由勸行殺、妄計方便等，這一切錯誤的作法稱為愚癡所生的殺生業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、不與取業道3　卯一、貪所生2　辰一、由饕餮</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不與取業道，說明不與取業道由貪瞋癡煩惱所生的情形，分三科；第一科貪所生，由貪煩惱所生的不與取業道，又分二科；第一科由饕餮，饕餮形容貪的樣子，貪財食而行不與取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4866"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若於他財食饕餮而取。是不與取，貪欲所生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，若是對於他人的財物、金錢、食品，以很貪心的、猶如狼吞虎嚥的樣子，將所貪的財物掠取來，這是由貪欲所生不與取的第一種情形。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》饕餮而取者：謂所不與、不捨、不棄而希望故。如本地分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/08.htm#48390:5738">陵本八卷十頁587</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　饕餮而取是說：他人所不給的物，名不與；不捨，是物的所有權是對方的，沒有布施捨出來；不棄，對方並沒有放棄物的所有權，對於這些財食心中希望取得，是從貪欲所生的不與取業道，如〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8，243頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、由劫盜</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由劫盜，由搶劫、偷盜而行不與取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或受他雇而行劫盜，或恩所攝、或祈後恩、或為衣食奉主教命、或為稱譽、或為安樂而行劫盜。如是一切不與取業，皆貪所生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或被他人雇用而行劫盜；或是被恩人要求去劫盜；或是期望劫盜以後對方會對自己好一點；或是為了衣食要聽主人的話而不與取；或是做了這件事，可得到他人的稱讚；或是為了生活能夠安樂而行劫盜。這一切不與取業，都是由貪欲所生不與取的第二種情形。有的小孩不懂事，會偷拿他人的東西，父母沒有馬上呵斥、糾正他，又鼓勵他的話，以後就不得了，越偷越多，甚至因此而喪失身命。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、瞋所生2　辰一、由惱害</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科瞋所生，由瞋煩惱所引發的劫盜，分二科；第一科由惱害，由惱害而劫盜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若作是思：彼於我所樂行無義，廣說乃至九惱害事增上力故，而行劫盜。不必貪著彼所有財，不必希求諸餘財物。是不與取，瞋恚所生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果自己作這樣的思惟：對方喜歡對自己做種種無義利的事，詳細說有九種會生起瞋惱的事，當對他們生起瞋心力量很強時，使用劫盜方式加諸於對方，並不是貪著對方的財，也不是希求其他的財物，純粹是要報復，要作弄對方，是由於惱害所產生的劫盜。這是由瞋煩惱所生不與取的第一種情形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、由憎他2　巳一、焚燒聚落等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由憎他，因為憎恨他人而劫盜，分二科；第一科焚燒聚落等，由焚燒聚落等成不與取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或憎他故，焚燒聚落舍宅財物珍玩資具，當知彼觸瞋恚所生，盜相似罪，或更增彊。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者只是因為很怨恨他人，就放了火將整個聚落、房舍、住宅、財物、珍寶、古玩、資生用具燒掉，這是瞋恚心所產生的強盜相似罪，或是比強盜更重的罪。因為這是將他人全部毀了，這是由瞋煩惱所生不與取的第二種情形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、令他劫奪等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科令他劫奪等，由令他劫奪等成不與取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4867"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或憎彼故，令他劫奪，破散彼財。他受教命依行事時，彼能教者不與取罪，從瞋恚生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於憎恨對方，就下令他人去劫奪、破壞散滅對方的財物；他人受到教導命令，就依教行事。這能教令的人，教導他人去做不與取的罪業是從瞋恚產生的，是由瞋煩惱所生不與取的第三種情形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、癡所生3　辰一、計為尊長</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科癡所生，是從癡煩惱所產生的不與取，分三科；第一科計為尊長，執著為尊長行劫盜，是正法而劫盜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若作是心：為尊長故而行劫盜，是為正法。名癡所生不與取罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果內心這樣想：去偷竊，是因為要供養尊長、父母、老師，認為這樣做是正法，因為自己有供養的心。這是錯誤的，是由愚癡所生的不與取罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、計由誹毀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科計由誹毀，由毀謗產生的不與取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或作是心：若有誹毀天梵世主，罵婆羅門，法應奪彼所有財物。此不與取亦從癡生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果內心這樣想：若是有人毀謗上天或者是毀謗梵天主：大梵天王，或是毀謗婆羅門種姓的人，理所當然應該要將誹毀者所有的財物都沒收，這種不與取罪也是從癡所生的。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、計為祠祀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科計為祠祀，為了祭祀劫盜他財成不與取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或作是心：若為祠祀、為祠祀支、為祠祀具，法應劫盜。是不與取亦從癡生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果作這樣想：若是為了祠祀、為祠祀相關的事、為祠祀用的資具，理所當然應該將對方的物品劫盜過來。這種不與取也是由癡所生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若為祠祀等者：謂如害為正法論者，為祠祀天而行劫盜，謂為是法，計所劫物為祠祀支、為祠祀具，害彼生命，得生天故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一種害為正法論者，認為若是了祭祀、拜神，而劫盜財物，是合法的。執著劫盜所得的財物，用來做祭祀的一個部分，做祭祀的資具，為祠祀而殺害畜生的生命是合法的，能令牠們生天。這也是由癡煩惱所產生的不與取，這是一種邪見。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、欲邪行業道3　卯一、貪所生3　辰一、由自貪纏</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科欲邪行業道，說明由三毒所生的欲邪行業道，分三科；第一科貪所生，貪煩惱所生的欲邪行業道，又分三科；第一科由自貪纏，由於自己有貪煩惱的現行而生的欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4868"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若有見聞不應行事，便不如理分別取相，遂貪欲纏之所纏縛而行非法，名貪所生欲邪行罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，若有人見到、或聽到不應該做的事，內心不如理取著分別這些相狀，於是被貪欲的煩惱現行所纏縛，而去做欲邪行非法的事，稱為貪所生的欲邪行罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、由受他雇</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由受他雇，由受他雇用而欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或受他雇竊行媒嫁，由此方便行所不行，彼便獲得貪欲所生欲邪行罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或是受他人的雇用，私底下做媒合嫁娶的事，由於能接近對方的方便，而做不應該做的欲邪行的事，因此獲得由貪欲所生的欲邪行罪。　</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、由多所為</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由多所為，由多種貪的因緣而作欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或欲攝受朋友知識，或為衣食承主教命，或為存活希求財穀金銀珍寶，而行邪行。如是一切，名貪所生欲邪行罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或是為了討好朋友、討好善知識，或者為了衣物飲食而奉承主人的教導命令，或者為了存活希望追求財穀金銀珍寶，而行邪行，如同以欲邪行為職業。這一切名為由貪所生的欲邪行罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、瞋所生2　辰一、為報怨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科瞋所生，由瞋煩惱所生的欲邪行，分二科；第一科為報怨，為報復故而行欲邪行。　</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若作是思：彼於我所樂行無義，廣說乃至九惱害事以為依止，而行邪行。非彼先有欲纏所纏，然於相違非所行事，為報怨故勉勵而行，名瞋所生欲邪行罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果內心這樣想：對方常常對自己及周邊相關的人作些不利的事，乃至依九種有情生起惱害事，為對方所做的事生起瞋心而去做欲邪行事，並不是在做欲邪行事之前，先有欲煩惱現行，而是對方違逆己意而做事，為了生氣報復，被激怒而做欲邪行的事。這是由瞋所生的欲邪行罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、為憎他</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科為憎他，為憎恨他人行欲邪行。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或憎彼故，以彼妻妾令他毀辱，彼若受教行欲邪行，便觸瞋恚所生相似欲邪行罪，或更尤重。如是一切欲邪行罪，名瞋所生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或為了憎恨他人，使令他人的妻妾受到他人的毀辱，受教唆的人若對教唆者所憎恨者的妻妾行欲邪行，使其受到毀辱，教唆者雖然自己沒有做，但是教唆他人做，也有瞋恚所生的相似欲邪行罪，或罪更重。這一切欲邪行罪，是瞋煩惱所生的欲邪行業道。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4869"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》便觸瞋恚所生相似欲邪行罪者：此欲邪行，由令他行，非自行故，由是故說觸相似罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　自己沒有做欲邪行，卻教唆他人去做，使令他人的妻女受到凌辱，或者是鼓勵他人凌辱其他人的妻女，因此說觸犯相似的罪業，這些事情也是欲邪行罪，甚至更重。佛法說自己不做請他人做，罪更嚴重。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、癡所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科癡所生，由愚痴煩惱所生的欲邪行。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若作是心，母及父親，或他婦女命為邪事，若不行者便獲大罪，若行此者便獲大福。非法謂法而行邪行，名癡所生欲邪行罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果內心這樣想：母親及父親，或者其他的婦女，要求自己做欲邪行的事，如果自己不照著做就有罪過，如果照著做就能獲大福報。因為是尊長要自己做的，愚癡的認為非法是如法的而行邪行，自己還沾沾自喜，認為是孝順父母，或是恭敬親友，這樣的邪因邪行，名為癡所生欲邪行罪。以上是說欲邪行業道的生因。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、妄語等業道2　卯一、舉妄語3　辰一、貪所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科妄語等業道，說明由三毒所生的妄語等業道，分二科；第一科舉妄語，舉妄語業道為例，又分三科；第一科貪所生，先說貪所生的妄語業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若為利養而說妄語，或怖畏他損己財物、或為稱譽、或為安樂而說妄語。如是一切，名貪所生妄語業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，若是為了名聞利養而說不實的話；或怖畏擔心他人損害自己的財物，告訴他人自己沒有錢，怕他人向自己借錢；或是為了得到他人的稱譽讚歎而說不實的話，自己並沒有禪定，卻常常去向師父說自己甚麼境界，以求師父讚歎；或是為了自己得安樂而說不實的話。這一切都是由貪所生的妄語業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、瞋所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科瞋所生，由瞋煩惱所生的妄語業道。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有依止九惱害事而說妄語，名瞋所生妄語業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果依止九種有情生起瞋心而說妄語，名為由瞋所生的妄語業道。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、癡所生3　巳一、計為尊長等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科癡所生，由愚癡煩惱所生的妄語業道，分三科；第一科計為尊長等，執著為尊長說妄語是合法，而說妄語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若作是心：為諸尊長、或復為牛、或為祠具，法應妄語。如是妄語，從癡所生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若作這種想法：為了尊敬的長輩、父母等、或是為持牛戒、或是為祭祀用品等原因，認為說妄語是合法的。由這些原因所說的妄語，都是從愚癡所生的妄語業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4870"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或復為牛者：謂有外道或持牛戒，計為清淨故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一些外道執著受持牛戒等便能得清淨解脫涅槃、出離生死、永超世間種種苦樂。又有一些外道在禪定裡面看到牛死後生天，就認為人應該要學牛吃草，以為吃草可以生天，告訴他人應該受持牛戒，牛怎麼做，人要跟著怎麼樣做，死後才能生天。如《俱舍論》說：合眼低頭，食草以為牛法。又有一類外道執著劫初時，成劫之初時，眾生福報很大，有地味生長，眾生所吃的，自然就有了，到儉劫時，地味消失，眾生很飢餓，上天為了哀憫眾生就化做牛身，為眾生耕田，使眾生可以繼續活下去，天的恩德很大，為生天說妄語沒有罪過。認為牛就是天的代表，牛的屎尿是清淨的，因為是上天化生的關係，這類為持牛戒所說的妄語，是從愚癡產生的妄語業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、計違諸天等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科計違諸天等，執著對違逆諸天等人說妄語，是合法的而說妄語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若作是心：諸有沙門、若婆羅門，違背諸天、違梵世主、違婆羅門，於彼妄語稱順正法。如是妄語，名癡所生妄語業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果內心這樣想：若有出家人或婆羅門，違背欲界天、違背大梵天王、違背婆羅門等，這樣的人不值得恭敬，對他們說妄語是合於正法的。這是與愚痴煩惱相應的妄語業道，這些妄語，稱為癡所生妄語業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、計無破僧罪</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科計無破僧罪，認為說妄語使僧團不和合，沒有罪過而說妄語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若作是計：於法法想，於毗奈耶毗奈耶想，以覆藏想妄語破僧，無有非法。如是妄語亦從癡生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果內心這樣想：認為妄語是合法合律，生起合法合律想，為了覆藏罪過而說妄語，破壞僧團和合，並不是非法。這種以覆藏想而說妄語也是從癡所生，其中有邪見。以上是說妄語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、例離間語等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例離間語等，例由於貪瞋癡所生的離間語、麤惡語，隨其所相應的，也是一樣。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如妄語業道，離間、麤惡二語業道，隨其所應，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同妄語業道，如是離間語、麤惡語二種業道，由貪瞋癡所生，隨其所相應的，跟妄語的情況也是一樣。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅五、綺語業道3　卯一、貪所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科綺語業道，能引無義的話是綺語，說明由貪瞋癡所生的綺語業道，分三科；第一科貪所生，由貪所生的綺語道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若為戲樂而行綺語，或為顯己是聰叡者而行綺語，或為財利稱譽安樂而行綺語，名貪所生綺語業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，若是為了戲樂、或為顯示自己有聰明才智、或是為了金錢利益、受到稱讚名譽、為自己的安樂，而說沒有義利的話，名為由貪所引生的綺語業道。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4871"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、瞋所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科瞋所生，由瞋所生的綺語業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有依止九惱害事而說綺語，名瞋所生綺語業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是為了九種有情受惱害事生起瞋心，而說沒有義利的話，名為瞋所生綺語業道。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、癡所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科癡所生，由癡所生的綺語業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有於中為求真實、為求堅固、為求出離、為求於法而行綺語，名癡所生綺語業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是有人認為說綺語，是為了追求真實的清淨涅槃、為了追求使生命、財產堅固，為了追求能夠出離苦惱，為了求法而說綺語，這是邪見愚癡所生的綺語業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅六、貪欲業道3　卯一、貪所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科貪欲業道，貪欲業道可由貪瞋癡三方面所引生，分三科；第一科貪所生，由貪所生起的貪欲業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若有於他非怨有情財物資具，先取其相，希望追求增上力故，起如是心：凡彼所有願當屬我。又從貪愛而生貪愛，名貪所生貪欲業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果對於與自己沒甚麼怨恨的一般有情所擁有的財物資具，先去了解它的內容，內心生起希望得到對方的財物資具的緣故，生起這種心：希望他的財物資具都能屬於自己。從貪愛資財而生起貪愛的虛妄分別，名為由貪所生的貪欲業道。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、瞋所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科瞋所生，由瞋所生起的貪欲業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於他財不計為好，但九惱事增上力故，起如是心：凡彼所有皆當屬我。又從瞋恚而生貪愛，名瞋所生貪欲業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果對於他人的財物並不覺得有什麼好，由於對方在九種有情受惱害事，使得自己生起瞋心，為了報復對方，生起這種想法：最好對方甚麼都沒有，對方的資財都歸屬於我。這是由瞋恚而生的貪欲業道，因為氣對方，希望對方的財富都歸自己，讓對方得不到好處，由瞋而生貪。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、癡所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科癡所生，是由癡所生的貪欲業道。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4872"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若作是計：諸有欲求魯達羅天、毗瑟笯天、釋梵世主眾妙世界，注心多住獲大福祐。作如是意注心多住，名癡所生貪欲業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果這樣想：凡是為追求，司掌風雨雷電的大自在天（魯達羅天），或是毗瑟天，或是帝釋與梵天，想要往生以後到那眾多微妙的世界，有種種的欲，乃至有定樂，心就安住在那裏，追求那種境界，認為這樣可以獲得很大的福報與庇佑，這種後有愛的貪欲，是名為癡所生的貪欲業道。因為這還是在三界生死輪迴中。毗瑟笯是幻化的意思，有的地方稱毗紐天，是梵天之母，是創造宇宙的最上神。釋梵是帝釋與梵天，帝釋是三十三天，梵是初禪天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅七、瞋恚業道3　卯一、貪所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科瞋恚業道，瞋恚業道也是由貪瞋癡三毒所引生，分三科；第一科是貪所生，由貪所生的瞋恚業道。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若為財利稱譽安樂，於他有情起損害心，非於彼所生怨憎想，謂彼長夜是我等怨。又從貪愛而生瞋恚，名貪所生瞋恚業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是為了財物、名利、稱歎、讚譽與安樂，對於其他有情生起想要損害的心，事實上心裡並不是怨憎對方，也不認為對方是自己的怨家，主要是為了貪愛財利稱譽安樂，才生起想要傷害對方的心情。這種是由貪欲所生的瞋恚業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、瞋所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科瞋所生，由瞋所生的瞋恚業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若九惱事增上力故，從怨對想起損害心，名瞋所生瞋恚業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果對方使自己因九種有情事增上的力量，生起怨恨的想法，進一步生起想要損害對方的心念，這是瞋所生的瞋恚業道。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、癡所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科癡所生，由癡所生的瞋恚業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若住此法及外道法，所有沙門、若婆羅門憎惡他見，於他見所及懷彼見沙門、婆羅門所起損害心，名癡所生瞋恚業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若安住在邪見及種種的外道法中，所有的出家人或婆羅門，憎恨厭惡與自己不同見解思想的人，對與自己不同見解思想的出家人或婆羅門生起損害心的想法，名為愚癡所生的瞋恚業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅八、邪見業道3　卯一、貪所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科邪見業道，邪見業道也由貪瞋癡所引生，分三科；第一科是貪所生，由貪所引生的邪見業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若作是心：諸有此見撥無施與，乃至廣說彼於王等獲大供養及衣服等。即以此義增上力故，起如是見，名貪所生邪見業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，由貪所生的邪見外道內心這樣想：認為沒有布施，善因不能招感樂果，乃至於自己可以從國王等處獲得大供養及衣服等。依止這種想法，生起這樣的見解，名為貪所生邪見業道。這種邪見是將自己貪求他人財物合理化，認為根本沒有布施行為的善因果，而理所當然的貪求他人的財物及供養。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、瞋所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科瞋所生，由瞋所引生的邪見業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4873"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若作是心：有施、有愛，乃至廣說如是見者違害於我，我今不應與怨同見。彼由憎恚，起如是見：無施、無愛，乃至廣說。名瞋所生邪見業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果這樣想：認為是有布施所得的功德，有愛護養育的功德，乃至種種合於因果見解的這類人，他們違害於我，我現在不應該與怨家有相同的見解。由於瞋恨對方，偏要跟對方有不一樣的見解，因此主張：沒有布施、沒有愛護養育的功德，而產生種種的邪見，名為瞋所生的邪見業道，由於瞋恨對方而產生不正確的思想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、癡所生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科癡所生，由愚癡所引生的邪見業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若不如理於法思惟、籌量、觀察，由此方便所引尋伺，發起邪見，名癡所生邪見業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種愚癡是外道本身的不如理作意，由於這類想法對於法的思惟、籌量、觀察，都是錯的，由無明影響發起邪見，名為愚癡所生的邪見業道。以上是由貪瞋癡三種煩惱產生十惡法的情況。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子七、決擇8　丑一、方便究竟4　寅一、殺生等業道2　卯一、舉殺生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科決擇，詳細決擇十不善業的各種情況，分八科；第一科方便究竟，說明十惡業道的方便與究竟，又分四科；第一科殺生等業道，說明殺生等業道，又分二科；第一科舉殺生，舉出殺生為例。第一科決擇的第一項重點是方便究竟，甚麼樣煩惱為造業的途徑，甚麼樣煩惱使業道究竟圓滿。究竟是指最常出現、最嚴重的、達到招感異熟果的程度。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，殺生業道三為方便，由瞋究竟。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，殺生業道由貪瞋癡三種煩惱引起殺生，而由瞋煩惱使殺生業道罪業圓滿。因為瞋心殺生時，使令所造的業更重，而達到圓滿的重業，由瞋使殺業究竟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、例麤語等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例麤語等，例麤語等業道，同殺生業道的由瞋究竟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如殺業道，麤語、瞋恚業道亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同殺生業道，麤惡語與瞋恚業道也是一樣，由貪瞋癡三種煩惱引起麤語、瞋恚業道，而由瞋煩惱使麤惡語及瞋恚業道罪業圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、不與取等業道2　卯一、舉不與取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不與取等業道，說明不與取等業道的方便與究竟，分二科；第一科舉不與取，舉出不與取為例。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不與取業道三為方便，由貪究竟。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不與取，偷盜業道以貪瞋癡三種煩惱為造業的途徑，最主要的煩惱是貪，由貪圓滿究竟不與取業道。通常會不與取，貪的情況是最多也是最嚴重的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、例邪行等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例邪行等，例舉邪行等業道，同不與取業道的由貪究竟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如不與取，邪行、貪欲業道亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同不與取，邪行與貪欲二種業道也是以貪瞋癡三種煩惱為造業的途徑，由貪究竟。雖然貪瞋癡都會產生不與取，邪行、貪欲業道，唯與貪煩惱相應的情況最多、最嚴重。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4874"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、除邪見所餘業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科除邪見所餘業道，除了邪見，所餘業道的方便與究竟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">除其邪見，所餘業道三為方便，由三究竟。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了邪見以外，邪見是癡為究竟，其他沒有說到的包括離間語、妄語這二種業道，是由貪瞋癡三法作為它的途徑，由貪瞋癡三種為究竟。貪瞋癡這幾種情況，都可能產生離間語、妄語，這種頻率都是相似的，都是很高的，為了貪、為了瞋、為了癡都會說出離間語或妄語，因此稱為由三究竟。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、邪見業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科邪見業道，邪見業的方便與究竟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">邪見業道三為方便，由癡究竟。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　邪見業道是錯誤的思想，由貪瞋癡產生，由癡煩惱圓滿究竟業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、依處4　寅一、殺生等業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依處，惡業生起的依止處，分四科；第一科殺生等業道，殺生等業道的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，殺生、邪行、妄語、離間、麤語、瞋恚，此六業道有情處起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，殺生、邪行、妄語、離間、麤惡語、瞋恚，這六種業道的依止處通常就是有情，對於有情才會作出這六種業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、不與取等業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不與取等業道，不與取等業道的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不與而取、貪欲業道，資財處起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不與取及貪欲業道的依止處是資財。由資具財產，才會產生偷盜及貪欲，前面的所緣境，殺生、邪行、妄語、離間語、麤惡語、瞋恚的所緣境是有情，不與取及貪欲的所緣境，主要是由於財物而引起的。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、綺語業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科綺語業道，綺語業道的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">綺語業道，名身處起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　綺語業道的依止處是由名身處起。名身，是指內心種種的名言分別。內心有很多名言、雜穢語、感情的這些話，依這些名言產生很多沒有義利的綺語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、邪見業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科邪見業道，邪見業道的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4875"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">邪見業道，諸行處起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　邪見業道，是依因緣所生的五蘊及器世間等一切有為法而生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、不善業道成極惡等4　寅一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科不善業道成極惡等，說明是甚麼使令不善業道成為極大的罪惡，分四科；第一科標，標出不善業道成極圓滿等的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，由三因緣，不善業道成極圓滿惡不善性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，有三種因緣使令不善業道，成為非常圓滿的惡不善性，將來一定會到地獄去受異熟果。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為三？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪三種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、自性過故；二、因緣過故；三、塗染過故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　使不善業道成為極圓滿惡不善性的三種因緣是：自性過、因緣的過失、塗染過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、釋3　卯一、自性過</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科自性過，說明不善業道成為圓滿的自性過失。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中殺生所引思，乃至邪見所引彼相應思，如是一切染汙性故、不善性故，由自性過說名為惡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不善業道中，從殺生所引思，乃至到邪見所引發的相應思心所，由於與十惡業相應的都是煩惱，引發思心所造業的煩惱欲樂都是染污的、是不善性的，使令不善業道成就圓滿惡不善性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》殺生所引思等者：此中殺生乃至邪見，皆約起彼欲樂為論，由是為先，思業現行故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十不善業中，做殺生乃至邪見的事時，都是由內心生起欲樂的變化，想要造業，先有煩惱的欲樂產生，使得思業現行造作。由與煩惱相應的邪欲與思業結合，這種染污性、不善性是它的自性過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、因緣過</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科因緣過，說明不善業道的因緣過失。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4876"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若以猛利貪欲、瞋恚、愚癡纏所發起，即此亦名由因緣過，成重惡性、成上不善，能引增上不可愛果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這十不善法的染污性、不善性體性本身就是有過失。造作時如果以猛利、強大的貪欲、瞋恚、愚癡現行煩惱與思心所相應，引發造作惡業，這也名為因緣過失，使不善業道成為極重惡性、成為上品的不善法，能引發種種增上的不可愛異熟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、塗染過2　辰一、出過失3　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科塗染過，說明不善業道由造業到究竟的塗染過失，分二科；辰一出過失，說明過失，又分三科；第一科標，標出由塗染過失，能引增上不可愛果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若到究竟，即此亦名由塗染過，成極重惡、成上不善，能引增上不可愛果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若造惡業到究竟圓滿時，如殺生業道，從頭到尾做完，對方也死了，稱為究竟。又如偷盜他人的財物，到手時稱作究竟，十惡業由造作開始到了圓滿究竟時，稱為塗染過失，使惡業成為極重的罪惡，成為上品的不善，而且能引發增上的不可愛果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若到究竟者：謂已成就究竟業道故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　到究竟，是指已經成就十不善的業道，已圓滿所造業事了。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是什麼原因？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有用染汙心，能引發他不可愛樂欣悅之苦，彼隨苦心威勢力故，能引發苦補特伽羅思，便觸得廣大之罪，是故名為塗染過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這件事是依被害眾生的苦來說。如果有染污心，能引發受害對象不可愛樂、不欣悅等種種內心的痛苦，加害者隨被害有情生起痛苦心的力量，能引發被害有情痛苦的感受、想法，便得到廣大的罪過，由被害有情內心的痛苦有多大，所造罪過就變成有多大，名為塗染過失。《瑜伽論記》說：雖然受害者並沒有詛咒加害者將來到地獄去，只是因為被殺害而覺得很痛苦，罪過就變成很大。這是依受害有情的苦受程度來決定所造罪的輕重，可見佛法蠻合道理的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、喻塗染3　巳一、磁石等喻2　午一、標法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科喻塗染，用比喻說明塗染過失，分三科；第一科磁石等喻，以磁石能吸引鐵來譬喻，又分二科；第一科標法，標出十惡業是能引苦的法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼雖不發如是相心：諸能引發我之苦者，當觸大罪。然彼法爾觸於大罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　約法相上或約法本身來說，雖然被害者沒有發這個心：能夠引發我的痛苦者，應該得到很大的罪過。由於加害有情這件事本身就是有過失的，自然得大罪過。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、喻合2　未一、舉磁石</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科喻合，引用譬喻合法，分二科；第一科舉磁石，舉出磁鐵為喻。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4877"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">譬如磁石雖不作意：諸所有鐵來附於我。然彼法爾所有近鐵，不由功用來附磁石。此中道理，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十惡業就像磁鐵。雖然磁鐵沒有作意：所有的鐵來依附在自己身上，然而只要磁鐵放在那裏，附近的鐵就自然會依附到這裡來。塗染過失的道理，應該知道也是一樣。加害者雖然沒有作意想要得到罪過，由於業性的染污性、不善性法爾如是，加害者作了這事，染污不善的罪過就自然會吸附上來，就像磁石附近的鐵。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例日珠等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例日珠等，例舉日珠等譬喻也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">日珠等喻，亦如是知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又如太陽照到以後，日珠就會出火了，也是可以了知。《瑜伽論記》卷17：喻中如有火珠待日光照即出火，故名為日珠。不論怎麼樣比喻，正面比喻或反面比喻，如果造了罪業，就算受害者不咒詛加害者會得到甚麼罪過，加害者自然有罪過，因為十惡業的染污不善自性，法爾是有罪過，就像磁石或是日珠一樣。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、大轉變喻2　午一、標法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科大轉變喻，大轉變的譬喻，又分二科；第一科標法，標出所造業會轉變的力量由來。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於思上無別有法，彼威力生來相依附，說名塗染。當知唯是此思轉變，由彼威力之所發起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又在思心所上並沒有其他的法，由於思心所的威力生起，使得業來依附於它，名為塗染。應當知道這是染污的思心所轉變所發起的威力，使罪業來依附，到究竟時，就有塗染過了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知唯是此思轉變等者：謂思轉變，唯由彼染汙心威力所發起故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　當與十不善法相應時，思心所會轉變，不善法的染污心本身就有威力，會發生這些罪過，這些罪過就來依附。思轉變成染污有大過失，稱作塗染。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》說：這裡的塗染過失，二乘戒重視身語業，沒有說到，大乘重視心念的思業，才說到這一點。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、引喻2　未一、舉業威勢緣力</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科引喻，引用譬喻說明，分二科；第一科舉業威勢緣力，舉出具有威勢的緣力，喻十不善業，法爾有力量得到過失。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如四大種業威勢力所生種種堅性、濕性、煖性、動性，非大種外別有如是種種諸性，然即大種業威勢緣，如是轉變。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同地水火風四大種的業用，具有種種的威勢力量，所生地堅、水濕、火暖、風動的體性，並不是離開地水火風以外另外有堅濕暖動的功能。這是大種本身具有威勢力量的緣故，能作這樣的轉變。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例神足加行緣力</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例神足加行緣力，例如神足加行緣力也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如業威勢緣力轉變，神足加行緣力轉變，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同業有威勢的緣力量轉變，當有神通時，由神通加行的緣力轉變，展現神通以後，也會產生種種的奇妙現象，應知也是如此。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、惡心轉變喻2　午一、舉喻</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一科惡心轉變喻，舉出惡心轉變譬喻塗染過，分二科；第一科舉喻，舉出譬喻說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4878"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又如魔王，惑媚無量娑梨藥迦諸婆羅門長者等心，令於世尊變異暴惡。非於彼心更增別法，說名惑媚。唯除魔王加行威勢生彼諸心，令其轉變成極暴惡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又如魔王，迷惑諂媚無量族村諸多的婆羅門長者，使令他們對於佛陀變心，產生暴惡的心情。魔王並不是在他們的心上更增加上別的法，名為惑媚。惑媚的根源是魔王的加行威勢，使令諸婆羅門長者等心，由過去所熏的煩惱種子引發現行，思心所被生起的煩惱染污，而生起對於佛陀的不敬心轉變為極暴惡。娑梨藥迦，這裡翻做族村，一族一族一村一村，稱族村。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、合法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科合法，以喻合法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中道理，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中的道理，應當知道也是如此。以上依譬喻主要在說離開惡思心所，沒有其他所謂殺害的事。相對來說，受佛所制定的戒之後，得到戒體為甚麼會有力量？也就是由於善思心所，法爾如是有防非止惡的力量，能招感可愛異熟。由染污思心所發動惡業，做了惡業又加強染污思的力量，雖然還沒有得到果報，對方也沒有咒詛你，可是惡業種子本身就有威力，還會展轉變異成熟，使造業者墮地獄。總之，十惡業以自性過為依止，若與強大的貪瞋癡相應就有因緣過，當惡業完成，形成極大的過惡，熏成惡思種子，展轉成熟，法爾招來惡趣異熟，便成塗染過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、定不定受業3　寅一、略辨二種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科定不定受業，說明十不善業之定不定受業，分三科；第一科略辨二種，要略說明二種。這段文主要決斷簡擇造了十不善業，是決定受業還是不決定受業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，如先所說作及增長業，若先所說由五因緣成極重業，名定受業。與此相違，名不定受業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如前面所說的作及增長業，造作十不善業內心還相續思惟，使得殺業成重，會決定受果報。前面所說的有五種因緣：由意樂故、由方便故、由無治故、由邪執故、由其事故，這些條件具足，便成極重業，一定是決定受業；如果五種因緣不具足，就不決定受業。其中無治是指沒有對治；其事是指所造業的對象。造了十不善業，若有對治，也可能重罪輕受，在懺文裡面常常這樣說：罪從心起將心懺，心若滅時罪亦亡，心亡罪滅兩俱空，是則名為真懺悔。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、標列四業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科標列四業，標示列舉出四種業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有四業。一、異熟定，二、時分定，三、二俱定，四、二俱不定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　約造業受果的情形，又開演成四種業：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、異熟定，決定會得到異熟果，所造十不善業如果很重，能招感地獄的異熟果，稱為異熟決定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、時分定，感果時間也決定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、二俱定，決定得果，時間也是一定的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、二俱不定，造業後，有被對治過了，有修行的道力、修禪定、或者修聖道，對治以後，感果時間不一定，也不一定會到地獄受果報，譬如成就初果的聖人，不會下地獄，以前做的殺生業，由於已對治、加上沒有因緣令它現起，是二俱不定的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、廣俱不定2　卯一、舉無學</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科廣俱不定，廣泛說明二種俱不定，分二科；第一科舉無學，舉出阿羅漢為例。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸阿羅漢所有不善決定受業，或於前生所作，或於此生先異生位所作，由少輕苦之所逼惱，便名果報已熟。若已轉依，果報種子皆永斷故，一切不受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又阿羅漢所有的過去所造不善決定受果報的業，或者是前生所做的，或者是今生於凡夫位時煩惱種子沒有斷除，曾造作十不善業，成就羅漢果以後，也會受到苦果，但是這種苦受的逼惱比較少，重罪輕受，這種果報就算成熟了。這是定受業所生果，因為這一生就入無餘涅槃了，受果時間不會延續到下一生，如果已經完全轉依，果報種子永遠斷除就不會受異熟果。成佛永遠轉依、果報種子永遠斷除時，一切就都不受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋所以</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋所以，解釋原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？由佛世尊依未解脫相續，建立定受業故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛陀為什麼說定受業，一定會受到果報？這是佛為了沒有解脫煩惱的有情，有煩惱作為增上緣，會繼續流轉生死，引生異熟果，決定會受果報，因此建立定受業。聖人阿羅漢的所有不善決定受業，包括宿生所造或此生在凡夫時所造的業成熟時，所感得的報也不會很重，因為阿羅漢已永遠斷除煩惱種子，沒有任何增上緣滋潤及引發過去所造的業種子，因此不會領受一切異熟果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4879"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑五、二業速轉2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科二業速轉，造業同時有二種加行，使二種業快速運轉，稱作二業速轉，分二科；第一科問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若於一時亦牽亦搦，盜取眾生，即斷其命。當言一業，為二業耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：若有人於一時做牽取偷盜家禽的事，接下來又殺害所偷盜的家禽，其所造的業是一種業還是二種業呢？牽，是指偷盜牽取。搦（音：溺），是指握或持，也就是握著殺害。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答3　卯一、標義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科標義，標出它的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：當言二業。以速轉故，於此二業，由增上慢，謂之為一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：應該說是造了二種不善業，包括不與取業、及殺業。由於造作時心念運轉得很快，做這件事時，先將他人的家禽牽取偷盜過來，接著再搦殺牠，其中第一念是偷盜，第二念是殺害。對於這二種不善業，由於錯誤認知，以為只有一種殺生業，或者認為只有一種偷盜業，那是錯的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、辨釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨釋，分辨解釋。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若謂我當牽彼，是第一思；即於盜時，復謂我當搦殺，是第二思。若時牽彼，爾時不搦；若時搦彼，爾時不牽；速疾轉故，生增上慢，謂是一時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果自己心裡這樣想：我應該將牠偷盜牽取過來，這是第一種思業；在偷盜時，又想：我應該要將牠殺掉，這是第二種思業。在偷盜牽取的當時，並沒有殺的念頭；在握殺的當時，並沒有偷盜財物；由於內心思念迅速，會錯認這一段時間，只有作一種業而已，事實上，已造作了二種業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、結成</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結成，結語成就二種業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故此中，當言二業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中應該說是造了二種業，這是謀財害命，先偷取他人的財物，再搦殺所取物命。經典上說這是二種惡業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由增上慢謂之為一者：當知此即錯亂境界所攝，由數錯亂起增上慢故。如本地分說應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/15.htm#48547:12766">陵本十五卷九頁1310</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的增上慢，是錯亂境界所攝，由數目有錯亂，導致錯認為只造了一種業。如〈本地分‧聞所成地〉卷15，551頁所說的數錯亂。以上是決擇二業速轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑六、現法受等2　寅一、辨因緣2　卯一、舉起善業5　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科現法受等，在現在的生命體裡面，作了業馬上會受到果報，說明十惡業之現法受等，分二科；第一科辨因緣，分辨得到現法受等的緣，又分二科；第一科舉起善業，舉出善業，又分五科；第一科標，標出成就現法受的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，略由三因緣故，成現法受業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，要略而言，由三種因緣的緣故，使所造作的業，成為現法受業，今生就會得到果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="60p4880"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為三？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪三種因緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、田廣大故；二、思廣大故；三、相續清淨故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種因緣由田廣大，由於福田很廣大，現在供養就馬上得到果報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種因緣由思廣大，內心的想法很殷重、很廣大、周全完備。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種因緣由相續清淨，修善法時沒有障礙，稱相續清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以布施為例，前生不曾障人布施，修布施時沒有障礙，布施前、布施後、布施當中都是很清淨的，自己也沒有執著，稱為相續清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、釋3　巳一、田廣大性3　午一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科田廣大性，福田廣大的體性為現法受業的因緣，又分三科；第一科總標，總體標出田成廣大性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="32812:48556"></a>由五種相，田成廣大。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於五種相貌 使布施的福田成為很廣大。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、列釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列釋，列出五相解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、從於一切有情第一利益安樂增上意樂住起，謂慈等至。二、從於一切有情第一將護他心住起，謂無諍等持。三、從第一寂靜涅槃樂相似聖住起，謂滅盡等至。四、已得一切不善不作律儀，謂預流果。五、極清淨相續究竟，謂阿羅漢及佛為首大苾芻僧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五種福田廣大的相貌：</span></span></span></div>
